commit 837d499149a1b442ceef124b826f00b8b0e43c50
Author: Ralf Schmitt <ralf@systemexit.de>
Date:   2013-11-11 17:02:15 +0100

    workaround 'first run' tox issue
    
    tox installs dependencies first, which includes mwlib.rl. mwlib.rl pulls
    in the last released version of mwlib. tox then installs the mwlib it
    has build from source without pip's -U flag, that is it won't update the
    installed version and we're basically testing against the last released
    version.
    
    we work around this issue by setting 'install_command', which requires
    a tox version later or equal 1.6.

1	0	tox.ini

    close stdin, stdout, stderr in init_tmp_cleaner
    
    this makes nslave recognize a bit faster that mw-render has finished
    since it won't wait for mw-render's child process - which just does an
    rmtree - to finish.

commit dae32f6b9c9a878c60133e0dc38b873522c7398f
Author: Ralf Schmitt <ralf@systemexit.de>
Date:   2013-05-13 12:18:48 +0200

    also fetch used images when fetching 'redirected revisions'
    
    when fetching by revision, and the revision points to a redirected
    page, we already did fetch the redirected page by title. we also need
    to call fetch_used for that title.
    
    here's an example metabook.json that revealed the bug:
    
    ,----[ metabook.json ]
    | {
    |     "items": [
    |         {
    |             "content_type": "text/x-wiki",
    |             "currentVersion": 1,
    |             "latest": 423796393,
    |             "revision": 423796393,
    |             "timestamp": "1302664603",
    |             "title": "ESRI grid",
    |             "type": "article",
    |             "url": "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ESRI_grid"
    |         }
    |     ],
    |     "licenses": [],
    |     "subtitle": "",
    |     "summary": "",
    |     "title": "GMS 2",
    |     "type": "collection",
    |     "version": 1,
    |     "wikis": [
    |         {
    |             "baseurl": "http://en.wikipedia.org/w/",
    |             "imagesize": 1200,
    |           "script_extension": ".php",
    |             "type": "wikiconf"
    |         }
    |     ]
    | }
    `----

1	0	mwlib/net/fetch.py

commit 2c1e08acd3af497a7d66c823555a76ad6e6386de
Author: Ralf Schmitt <ralf@systemexit.de>
Date:   2013-03-27 12:28:35 +0100

    fix redirect handling when using 'expandtemplates'
    
    the redirect handling has been broken as part of 'expandtemplates'
    change. I.e. we do store the pages under their original non-redirected
    name and therefor we can't look them up under their redirected name.
    
    we now try both names, the original and the redirected one.
    
    I'm not quite sure what goes wrong if I remove redirect handling
    completely when fetching. So, I didn't do that.

1	3	mwlib/net/fetch.py
10	3	mwlib/nuwiki.py

commit 70680353b768348fd5c76ade3abf7fb87a94703a
Author: Ralf Schmitt <ralf@systemexit.de>
Date:   2012-05-08 11:55:37 +0200

    unconditionally require simplejson
    
    the builtin json module loads json strings as unicode strings. these
    get passed as keyword arguments. python < 2.6.5 can't handle that.
    So, we require a recent simplejson module as a workaround.

commit 2680912f7f4719b65188af8c54505684d9bd8340
Author: Ralf Schmitt <ralf@systemexit.de>
Date:   2011-10-06 01:14:30 +0200

    count number of jobs for progress before they have been scheduled
    
    when fetching collections with a large number of articles this gives
    much better progress since _refcall might block.  we do this by having
    a _refcall_noinc method which doesn't count the newly added job and by
    adding to count_total directly.

commit fd80635ad6817faafded7372ab8c39a5a327102c
Author: Ralf Schmitt <ralf@systemexit.de>
Date:   2011-10-06 00:41:24 +0200

    allow the dispatcher greenlet to be killed
    
    'except Exception' catches GreenletExit, which is not quite what we
    wanted. This commit fixes a deadlock when trying to kill the
    dispatcher greenlet (gevent.hub.LoopExit: This operation would block
    forever).

commit f460c4bcd63d09e6cf38bdfda219ba5d4b6b8462
Author: Ralf Schmitt <ralf@systemexit.de>
Date:   2011-10-05 23:18:05 +0200

    prevent deadlocks in _decref
    
    _decref is called by a greenlet from the refcall_pool. Calling
    dispatch directly may deadlock, cause it may try to spawn some more
    greenlets in that pool. We now use events instead and a dedicated
    greenlet that just calls dispatch in a loop when the event is set.

22	7	mwlib/net/fetch.py

commit 51663fb811160e76e57bdbd2a6a673c00a9bbc9e
Author: Ralf Schmitt <ralf@systemexit.de>
Date:   2011-10-04 22:20:56 +0200

    use gevent instead of twisted in mw-zip/mw-render
    
    This makes some of the code quite a bit cleaner and allows me to
    remove some of the horrible hacks I've been using. Unfortunately I
    also had to change a lot of code.
    
    It also adds two new dependencies to mwlib (greenlet, gevent) and
    removes one (twisted).
    
    mw-zip and mw-render use gevent's monkey.patch_all to make urllib2
    cooperative.
    
    net.mwapi has been completely replaced with net.sapi, the twisted
    podclient class is gone.

commit ab12b01e6feb071bb0d5d784dc50c5c28cedfa64
Author: Ralf Schmitt <ralf@systemexit.de>
Date:   2011-10-04 14:02:26 +0200

    limit the maximum number of simultaneous calls to fetch_pages
    
    mwapi.fetch_pages currently schedules more HTTP GETs. When calling
    mwapi.fetch_pages for lots of pages, most of the calls are running
    cause the HTTP GETs scheduled are pushed to the end of the scheduling
    list. That's fine -- unless you're optimizing memory usage.
